### [183] [Asymmetric Nash Seeking via Best Response Maps: Global Linear Convergence and Robustness to Inexact Reaction Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.17058)
*Mahdis Rabbani,Navid Mojahed,Shima Nazari*

Main category: cs.GT

TL;DR: 该论文提出了一种针对信息不对称的两人约束博弈的梯度下降-最优响应迭代算法，在玩家2仅通过最优响应映射可用的情况下，证明了纳什均衡的存在唯一性及算法的全局线性收敛性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统纳什均衡求解方法通常假设所有玩家都了解彼此的优化目标和约束条件，这在实践中往往不现实。论文旨在解决信息不对称的两人约束博弈问题，其中玩家1了解自身目标函数和约束，而玩家2仅通过最优响应映射可用。

Method: 提出了一种非对称投影梯度下降-最优响应迭代算法，该算法不需要玩家之间完全了解彼此的优化问题。算法结合了玩家1的投影梯度下降和玩家2的最优响应映射，在适当正则性条件下分析了精确和近似最优响应映射两种情况。

Result: 在精确最优响应映射下，证明了纳什均衡的存在性和唯一性，并建立了算法的全局线性收敛性。在近似最优响应映射情况下，当近似误差有界时，证明了迭代序列会进入真实纳什均衡的O(ε)邻域内。数值实验验证了收敛行为和误差缩放特性。

Conclusion: 该研究为信息不对称的约束博弈提供了一种实用的均衡求解框架，放宽了对玩家间完全信息共享的要求，在最优响应映射精确或近似的情况下都具有理论保证，适用于实际应用中玩家信息不完全可得的场景。

Abstract: Nash equilibria provide a principled framework for modeling interactions in multi-agent decision-making and control. However, many equilibrium-seeking methods implicitly assume that each agent has access to the other agents' objectives and constraints, an assumption that is often unrealistic in practice. This letter studies a class of asymmetric-information two-player constrained games with decoupled feasible sets, in which Player 1 knows its own objective and constraints while Player 2 is available only through a best-response map. For this class of games, we propose an asymmetric projected gradient descent-best response iteration that does not require full mutual knowledge of both players' optimization problems. Under suitable regularity conditions, we establish the existence and uniqueness of the Nash equilibrium and prove global linear convergence of the proposed iteration when the best-response map is exact. Recognizing that best-response maps are often learned or estimated, we further analyze the inexact case and show that, when the approximation error is uniformly bounded by $\varepsilon$, the iterates enter an explicit $O(\varepsilon)$ neighborhood of the true Nash equilibrium. Numerical results on a benchmark game corroborate the predicted convergence behavior and error scaling.

</details>


### [184] [Adaptive Contracts for Cost-Effective AI Delegation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.17212)
*Eden Saig,Tamar Garbuz,Ariel D. Procaccia,Inbal Talgam-Cohen,Jamie Tucker-Foltz*

Main category: cs.GT

TL;DR: 论文提出自适应合同用于AI委托，通过选择性详细评估来平衡评估噪声与成本，提供高效算法并证明其优于非自适应基线。

Motivation: 当组织通过按绩效付费合同将文本生成任务委托给AI提供商时，评估噪声会导致预期支付增加。随着评估方法变得更加复杂，减少噪声的经济效益往往被增加的评估成本所抵消。

Method: 引入自适应合同，允许在观察初始粗略信号后选择性地进行详细评估以节省资源。提供计算最优自适应合同的高效算法，证明一般情况下的近似难度，提出随机化自适应合同模型，并在问答和代码生成数据集上进行实证评估。

Result: 在自然假设或核心问题维度较小时提供高效算法，证明一般非结构化情况的近似难度。实证结果表明自适应方法在问答和代码生成任务上优于非自适应基线。

Conclusion: 自适应合同能有效平衡AI委托中的评估噪声与成本，通过选择性详细评估实现资源节约，在现实任务中展现出优于传统非自适应方法的性能。

Abstract: When organizations delegate text generation tasks to AI providers via pay-for-performance contracts, expected payments rise when evaluation is noisy. As evaluation methods become more elaborate, the economic benefits of decreased noise are often overshadowed by increased evaluation costs. In this work, we introduce adaptive contracts for AI delegation, which allow detailed evaluation to be performed selectively after observing an initial coarse signal in order to conserve resources. We make three sets of contributions: First, we provide efficient algorithms for computing optimal adaptive contracts under natural assumptions or when core problem dimensions are small, and prove hardness of approximation in the general unstructured case. We then formulate alternative models of randomized adaptive contracts and discuss their benefits and limitations. Finally, we empirically demonstrate the benefits of adaptivity over non-adaptive baselines using question-answering and code-generation datasets.

### [185] [A mechanism design overview of Sedna](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.17614)
*Benjamin Marsh,Alejandro Ranchal-Pedrosa*

Main category: cs.GT

TL;DR: Sedna协议存在激励失败问题：提案者联盟可扣留交易符号包，延迟链上解码。论文提出PIVOT-K奖励机制和自适应发送者策略来解决此问题，显著降低MEV成本。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究Sedna这类编码多提案者共识协议中的激励失败问题。当提案者联盟扣留交易符号包时，会延迟链上解码过程，同时私下汇集缺失符号，从而获得信息优势并可能进行MEV提取。

Method: 1. 分析联盟扣留行为对符号累积延迟的影响，使用KL型大偏差界限表征延迟概率；2. 提出PIVOT-K奖励机制，将奖励集中在实际触发解码的κ个符号包上；3. 设计自适应发送者"棘轮"策略，排除未兑现票据的通道；4. 推导部分和联盟偏差下的激励兼容条件。

Result: 1. 当松弛度Δ=0时存在"刀刃病理"：扣留单个符号包就能以高概率将包含延迟到下一个时隙；2. PIVOT-K机制能有效对抗部分和联盟偏差；3. 自适应棘轮策略将多时隙扣留压缩为第一个时隙的缺陷，将所需奖励降低数个数量级；4. 对于现实参数，Sedna可将MEV成本降至交易价值的0.04%。

Conclusion: 通过PIVOT-K奖励机制和自适应发送者策略，Sedna协议能够有效解决提案者联盟扣留符号包的激励失败问题，显著降低MEV成本，实现高吞吐量和"直到解码"隐私保护的设计目标。

Abstract: Sedna is a coded multi-proposer consensus protocol in which a sender shards a transaction payload into rateless symbols and disseminates them across parallel proposer lanes, providing high throughput and ``until decode'' privacy. This paper studies a sharp incentive failure in such systems. A cartel of lane proposers can withhold the bundles addressed to its lanes, slowing the chain's symbol accumulation while privately pooling the missing symbols. Because finalized symbols become public, the cartel's multi-slot information lead is governed by a chain level delay event where the chain fails to accumulate the $κ$ bundles needed for decoding by the honest horizon $t^\star=\lceil κ/m\rceil$. We characterize the resulting delay probability with KL-type large deviation bounds and show a knife edge pathology when the slack $Δ=t^\star m-κ$ is zero such that withholding a single bundle suffices to push inclusion into the next slot with high probability.
  We propose \textsf{PIVOT-$K$}, a Sedna native pivotal bundle bounty that concentrates rewards on the $κ$ bundles that actually trigger decoding, and we derive explicit incentive compatibility conditions against partial and coalition deviations. We further show that an adaptive sender ``ratchet'' that excludes lanes whose tickets were not redeemed collapses multi-slot withholding into a first slot deficit when $t^\star\ge 2$, reducing the required bounty by orders of magnitude. We close by bounding irreducible within slot decode races and providing parameter guidance and numerical illustrations. Our results show that for realistic parameters Sedna can reduce MEV costs to 0.04\% of the transaction value.

</details>


### [186] [Stronger core results with multidimensional prices](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.17862)
*Mark Braverman,Jingyi Liu,Eric Xue,Chenghan Zhou*

Main category: cs.GT

TL;DR: 提出带有多维价格的广义竞争均衡概念，解决无货币单边匹配市场中均衡可能不存在的问题，证明其始终存在且位于拒绝核心内，并展示核心收敛性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在无货币的单边匹配市场中，传统竞争均衡可能不存在，强核心可能为空。Hylland和Zeckhauser(1979)已指出这一问题，需要新的解决方案来保证稳定分配的存在性。

Method: 提出广义竞争均衡概念，为每个物品分配多维价格而非单一标量价格。证明该均衡始终存在且位于拒绝核心内，拒绝核心稳定性强于弱核心稳定性。通过经济规模增长分析，展示拒绝核心向多维价格竞争均衡集合的收敛性。

Result: 多维价格竞争均衡始终存在，且位于拒绝核心内。拒绝核心稳定性严格强于弱核心稳定性。当经济规模增长时，拒绝核心收敛于多维价格竞争均衡集合，在无饱和性假设下实现核心收敛。

Conclusion: 多维价格竞争均衡为解决无货币单边匹配市场的均衡存在性问题提供了有效方案，其始终存在且具有更强的稳定性保证，并在大规模经济中收敛于传统竞争均衡概念。

Abstract: We study one-sided matchings with endowments in the absence of money. It is well-known that a competitive equilibrium may not always exist and that the strong core may be empty in this setting [Hylland and Zeckhauser, 1979]. We propose a generalization of competitive equilibria that associates each item with a multi-dimensional price. We show that this solution concept always exists and resides within the rejective core [Konovalov, 2005]. Rejective core stability is strictly stronger than weak core stability: allocations in the rejective core are elements of the weak core, but the opposite is not true. Moreover, we show that the rejective core always converges to the set of competitive equilibria with multi-dimensional prices as the economy grows, demonstrating core convergence in a setting without non-satiation.

</details>

### [187] [A scalable neural bundle map for multiphysics prediction in lithium-ion battery across varying configurations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.17209)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有计算框架难以捕捉不同电池几何结构和操作条件下的电化学-热-机械耦合动力学，需要一种能处理几何多样性并保持物理定律一致性的高效预测方法。

Method: 提出神经丛映射（NBM）框架，将多物理场演化重新表述为几何基流形上的丛映射，实现几何复杂性与物理定律的完全解耦，确保不同域间的强算子连续性。

Result: NBM实现了高保真时空预测，归一化平均绝对误差小于1%，长时程预测稳定，计算成本比传统求解器降低两个数量级；快速探索配置空间发现能量密度提升38%的最优设计；通过少样本迁移学习展示多电池系统的可扩展性。

Conclusion: NBM为复杂储能系统的智能设计和实时监控提供了基础范式，通过数学严谨的框架解决了多物理场预测中的几何多样性挑战，在精度、效率和可扩展性方面均取得显著突破。

Abstract: Efficient and accurate prediction of Multiphysics evolution across diverse cell geometries is fundamental to the design, management and safety of lithium-ion batteries. However, existing computational frameworks struggle to capture the coupled electrochemical, thermal, and mechanical dynamics across diverse cell geometries and varying operating conditions. Here, we present a Neural Bundle Map (NBM), a mathematically rigorous framework that reformulates multiphysics evolution as a bundle map over a geometric base manifold. This approach enables the complete decoupling of geometric complexity from underlying physical laws, ensuring strong operator continuity across varying domains. Our framework achieves high-fidelity spatiotemporal predictions with a normalized mean absolute error of less than 1% across varying configurations, while maintaining stability during long-horizon forecasting far beyond the training window and reducing computational costs by two orders of magnitude compared with conventional solvers. Leveraging this capability, we rapidly explored a vast configurational space to identify an optimal battery design that yields a 38% increase in energy density while adhering to thermal safety constraints. Furthermore, the NBM demonstrates remarkable scalability to multi-cell systems through few-shot transfer learning, providing a foundational paradigm for the intelligent design and real-time monitoring of complex energy storage infrastructures.

Here, we will present its application to generate efficient algebraic multigrid methods with so-called \emph{flexible cycling}, that is, level-specific smoothing sequences and non-recursive cycling patterns. The search space with such non-standard cycles is intractable to navigate manually, and is generated using genetic programming (GP) guided by context-free grammars. Numerical experiments with the linear algebra library, \emph{hypre}, demonstrate the potential of these non-standard GP cycles to improve multigrid performance both as a solver and a preconditioner.

Abstract: H Infinity robust control synthesis for gust load alleviation of very flexible aircraft is presented. ### [190] [Adaptive Encoding Strategy for Quantum Annealing in Mixed-Variable Engineering Optimization](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.17506)
*Fabian Key,Lukas Freinberger,Mayu Muramatsu,Norbert Hosters*

Main category: cs.CE

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种用于量子退火中连续变量的自适应编码策略，以解决混合离散-连续优化问题，在固定二进制变量预算下提高了求解质量。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 混合离散-连续优化在工程设计中至关重要，但量子退火的原生二进制特性仅支持离散变量。现有方法要么将耦合问题拆分（牺牲量子退火的全局搜索优势），要么使用固定位深编码（可能低估动态范围或增加二进制变量数量）。研究表明，简单地增加位深甚至可能降低当前量子退火硬件的性能，因此需要替代编码方法。

Method: 提出了一种用于量子退火中连续变量的自适应编码策略，包括可表示范围更新策略。将其集成到结构设计优化的最小互补能量公式中，形成一个单一的耦合约束问题。采用二次惩罚方法，在更新连续变量表示的同时针对完整原始目标，保持量子退火的全局搜索能力。

Result: 在复合材料杆尺寸优化的已发表基准测试中，自适应编码在固定二进制变量预算下提高了求解质量，展示了优越的精度-资源权衡。

Conclusion: 该框架超越了结构设计领域，为量子退火中的连续变量编码提供了实用指导，表明自适应表示可以增强当前硬件的精度。

Abstract: Mixed discrete-continuous optimization is central to engineering design, where discrete choices interact with continuous fields. These problems are difficult due to high-dimensional, complex search spaces. To tackle them, Quantum Annealing (QA) is promising, yet its native binary nature supports only discrete variables, making accurate and efficient encodings of continuous quantities a central challenge. Existing approaches either split the coupled problem, mapping discrete decisions to QA while solving continuous fields classically, or use fixed-bit-depth encodings. The former compromises QA's global search advantages; the latter can underrepresent dynamic range or inflate the number of binary variables. We show that simply increasing bit depth can even degrade performance on current QA hardware, underscoring the need for alternative encodings. In response, we introduce an adaptive encoding strategy for continuous variables in QA that enables efficient treatment of coupled mixed-variable problems. We propose an update strategy for the representable ranges of the continuous variables and demonstrate its utility by integrating it into the minimum complementary energy formulation for structural design optimization, which provides a single, coupled constrained problem. We apply a quadratic penalty method where we update the representation of the continuous variables while targeting the full original objective, preserving QA's global search capability. On a published benchmark, the size optimization of a composite rod, our adaptive encoding improves solution quality under a fixed binary variable budget, demonstrating a superior precision-resource trade-off. Since the framework generalizes beyond structural design, it offers practical guidance for encoding continuous variables for QA and indicates that adaptive representations can enhance precision on current hardware.

</details>


### [191] [Training Diffusion Language Models for Black-Box Optimization](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.17919)
*Zipeng Sun,Can Chen,Ye Yuan,Haolun Wu,Jiayao Gu,Christopher Pal,Xue Liu*

Main category: cs.CE

TL;DR: 提出使用扩散语言模型进行离线黑盒优化，通过统一提示-响应语料库和两阶段后训练框架，在Design-Bench小数据设置上取得SOTA结果


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 离线黑盒优化在机器人、DNA和材料科学中很重要，但现有自回归语言模型难以捕捉设计问题中的强双向依赖关系，而扩散语言模型具有双向建模能力但存在领域差距

Method: 1) 构建统一提示-响应语料库并使用分隔符标记字段边界；2) 两阶段后训练框架：第一阶段通过掩码响应预测进行监督微调，第二阶段采用基于标签改进奖励的强化学习

Result: 在Design-Bench小数据设置上取得了最先进的结果

Conclusion: 扩散语言模型通过适当的领域适应和训练策略，能够有效解决离线黑盒优化问题，特别适合具有强双向依赖关系的设计任务

Abstract: We study offline black-box optimization (BBO), aiming to discover improved designs from an offline dataset of designs and labels, a problem common in robotics, DNA, and materials science with limited labeled samples. While recent work applies autoregressive LLMs to BBO by formatting tasks as natural-language prompts, their left-to-right design generation struggles to capture the strong bidirectional dependencies inherent in design problems. To address this, we propose adapting diffusion LLMs to offline BBO to leverage their bidirectional modeling capabilities. However, a domain gap exists between the natural text pre-training of diffusion LLMs and the heterogeneous signals in BBO (prompts, designs, and labels). To bridge this gap, we construct a unified prompt-response corpus and introduce delimiter tokens to explicitly mark field boundaries for domain adaptation. We further propose a two-stage post-training framework to align the diffusion LLM generation with high-label designs. The first stage performs supervised fine-tuning on the unified dataset via masked-response prediction, and the second stage adopts reinforcement learning with rewards defined by label improvements. Our method achieves state-of-the-art results on Design-Bench small-data settings.
